اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَهْتِكُ الْعِصَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ النِّقَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُغَيِّرُ النِّعَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَحْبِسُ الدُّعَاءَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ الْبَلَاءَ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أَتَوَجَّهُ إِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَآلِهِ، وَبِأَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ الطَّيِّبِينَ الطَّاهِرِينَ.  
يَا وَجِيهًا عِنْدَ اللهِ، اِشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ اللهِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، اقْبَلْ دُعَائِي، وَاسْمَعْ نِدَائِي، وَاقْضِ حَاجَتِي.

السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللهِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكِ يَا فَاطِمَةُ الزَّهْرَاءُ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى جَعْفَرِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُوسَى بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُوسَى، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحُجَّةِ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ.

رَبِّ زِدْنِي عِلْمًا.  
رَبِّ اشْرَحْ لِي صَدْرِي، وَيَسِّرْ لِي أَمْرِي، وَاحْلُلْ عُقْدَةً مِنْ لِسَانِي، يَفْقَهُوا قَوْلِي.  
رَبَّنَا لَا تُزِغْ قُلُوبَنَا بَعْدَ إِذْ هَدَيْتَنَا، وَهَبْ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ رَحْمَةً، إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ الْوَهَّابُ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أَسْأَلُكَ فَهْمَ النَّبِيِّينَ، وَحِفْظَ الْمُرْسَلِينَ، وَإِلْهَامَ الْمَلَائِكَةِ الْمُقَرَّبِينَ، وَنُورًا فِي الْقَلْبِ، وَصَفَاءً فِي الذِّهْنِ، وَسَدَادًا فِي الْقَوْلِ وَالْعَمَلِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلِ الْعِلْمَ نُورًا لَا حِجَابًا، وَزِدْنِي بِهِ تَوَاضُعًا وَعَمَلًا صَالِحًا، وَافْتَحْ عَلَيَّ أَبْوَابَ الْحِكْمَةِ وَالْبَصِيرَةِ وَحُسْنِ الْفَهْمِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ صَفِّ ذِهْنِي مِنَ التَّشْوِيشِ، وَثَبِّتْ قَلْبِي عِنْدَ الْقِرَاءَةِ وَالْمُذَاكَرَةِ، وَبَارِكْ لِي فِي وَقْتِي، وَاجْعَلْ سَعْيِي فِي طَلَبِ الْعِلْمِ مَشْكُورًا.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ يَسِّرْ لِي مَا صَعُبَ مِنَ الدُّرُوسِ، وَقَرِّبْ لِي مَا بَعُدَ مِنَ الْفَهْمِ، وَارْزُقْنِي حُسْنَ الْحِفْظِ وَسُرْعَةَ التَّذَكُّرِ وَصِدْقَ الْجَوَابِ عِنْدَ الْحَاجَةِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْ لِي فِي الِامْتِحَانِ سَكِينَةً وَتَوْفِيقًا، وَفِي الدِّرَاسَةِ نَشَاطًا وَثَبَاتًا، وَفِي الْعَاقِبَةِ نَجَاحًا مَقْرُونًا بِرِضَاكَ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي لَا أَسْأَلُكَ نَجَاحًا بِظُلْمِ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا بِسَلْبِ حَقِّ أَحَدٍ، وَلَا بِنُقْصَانِ رِزْقِ أَحَدٍ، وَلَكِنْ أَسْأَلُكَ فَضْلًا مِنْ عِنْدِكَ، وَتَوْفِيقًا لَا يَضُرُّ عَبْدًا مِنْ عِبَادِكَ.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ إِنِّي كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ.  
حَسْبُنَا اللهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ كُنْ لِوَلِيِّكَ الْحُجَّةِ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ، صَلَوَاتُكَ عَلَيْهِ وَعَلَى آبَائِهِ، فِي هٰذِهِ السَّاعَةِ وَفِي كُلِّ سَاعَةٍ، وَلِيًّا وَحَافِظًا وَقَائِدًا وَنَاصِرًا وَدَلِيلًا وَعَيْنًا، حَتَّى تُسْكِنَهُ أَرْضَكَ طَوْعًا، وَتُمَتِّعَهُ فِيهَا طَوِيلًا.

قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ، اللهُ الصَّمَدُ، لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.  
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الْفَلَقِ، مِنْ شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ النَّفَّاثَاتِ فِي الْعُقَدِ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ.  
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ، مَلِكِ النَّاسِ، إِلٰهِ النَّاسِ، مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ، الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ، مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ، وَالْمُسْلِمِينَ وَالْمُسْلِمَاتِ، الْأَحْيَاءِ مِنْهُمْ وَالْأَمْوَاتِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ اجْعَلْ ثَوَابَ مَا قُرِئَ وَدُعِيَ هَدِيَّةً إِلَى النَّبِيِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِهِ الطَّاهِرِينَ، وَإِلَى أَرْوَاحِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ، وَزِدْهُمْ رَحْمَةً وَرِضْوَانًا.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنَّ الْعِبَادَ عِبَادُكَ، وَالْأَمْرَ أَمْرُكَ، وَالنَّفْعَ وَالضُّرَّ بِيَدِكَ وَحْدَكَ لَا شَرِيكَ لَكَ؛ فَاجْعَلْ تَوَسُّلِي بِمُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ تَوَسُّلًا إِلَيْكَ بِمَنْ أَكْرَمْتَهُمْ، وَلَا تَكِلْنِي إِلَى غَيْرِكَ طَرْفَةَ عَيْنٍ أَبَدًا.  
رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ، وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَاخْتِمْ لَنَا بِالْخَيْرِ، وَاجْعَلْ دُعَاءَنَا مَرْفُوعًا، وَذَنْبَنَا مَغْفُورًا، وَسَعْيَنَا مَشْكُورًا.  
وَآخِرُ دَعْوَانَا أَنِ الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.

---

## שומרונים

בשם יהוה אלהינו, אל עולם.

שמע ישראל: יהוה אלהינו יהוה אחד.  
ואהבת את יהוה אלהיך בכל לבבך ובכל נפשך ובכל מאדך.  
והיו הדברים האלה אשר אנכי מצוך היום על לבבך.  
ושננתם לבניך ודברת בם בשבתך בביתך ובלכתך בדרך ובשכבך ובקומך.

יהוה ימלך לעלם ועד.  
בהר גריזים בחר יהוה לשכן שמו שם.

יהוה אלהי אברהם אלהי יצחק ואלהי יעקב,  
פתח לבי לתורת משה, ותן בי חכמה ודעת ובינה.  
זכך מחשבותי, וישר לבבי, והסר ממני בלבול ופחד ושקר.  
חזק ידי בלימוד ובקריאה ובכתיבה, למען אתקדם בדרכי הטוב.  
ביום מבחן ובשעת שאלה, תן לי לב שומע, זכרון נכון, ושכל בהיר.  
אל אבקש לקחת ברכת איש ולא להמעיט חלקו;  
כי אם ברכה ישרה, חכמה, שלום, ועמל נאמן לפניך.

יברכך יהוה וישמרך.  
יאר יהוה פניו אליך ויחנך.  
ישא יהוה פניו אליך וישם לך שלום.

יהוה אלהינו יהוה אחד;  
תורת משה אמת, והר גריזים מקום ברכה.  
שמור פי ולבי מן קסם ומן שקר,  
והעמדני לפניך בשלום וביושר.

אמן.

---

## AMORC 玫瑰十字会

Pax Profunda.

God of my Heart, God of my Realization,  
I enter the silence in humility, sincerity, and service.

May the Cosmic attune the Inner Self  
to Light, Life, and Love.

Lux. Vita. Amor.

For the increase of wisdom in study and learning,  
for clarity of mind, steady attention, rightful memory,  
favorable examination fortune, and true progress in scholarship,  
let only that which is lawful, compassionate, harmonious,  
and in accord with the highest good be established.

May understanding arise without pride.  
May diligence be strengthened without anxiety.  
May success come without depriving another of blessing, opportunity, or rightful merit.  
May knowledge be used in service, tolerance, and goodwill.

AUM.  
AUM.  
AUM.

May peace profound abide in the mind and heart.  
May wisdom guide every lesson, review, examination, and decision.  
May harmony be restored where harmony is rightful.  
May all selfishness, coercion, fear, confusion, and harmful intention be dissolved.

Pax Profunda.

Lux, Vita, Amor.

AUM.

---

## یارسان / اهل حق

Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق.

Niyyat-e īn duʿā va yād kardān:  
barā-ye roshd-e dānesh va kherad dar dars va ketāb,  
barā-ye rowshanī-ye del o zehn,  
barā-ye gushāyesh-e rāh-e emtehān,  
va barā-ye pīshraft-e pāk dar ʿelm o āmūzesh,  
dar rāh-e Yārī,  
bā pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā.

Pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā.  
پاکی، راستی، نیستی، رضا.

Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق، یا حق، یا حق.

Dar īn jam-e yād,  
niyāz-e del barā-ye dānāyī ast;  
har nām va har sukhan rā be Ḥaqq mī-sepārīm.  
Na az kasī kamī mī-khāhīm,  
na haqq-e dīgarān rā mī-gīrīm;  
gushāyesh rā dar rāstī va ʿadl mī-jūyīm.

Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق.

Kalām-khwānī-e ʿalānī dar yād-e Kalām-e Saranjām:  
bā del-e pāk, bā zabān-e rāst,  
bā nīstī-ye nafs, bā riḍā-ye jān,  
nūr-e fahm bar ketāb o dars betābad,  
ḥāfeẓe ārām gardad,  
andīshe safā yābad,  
va qadam dar rāh-e Yārī ostovār mānad.

Yā Ḥaqq.  
Yā Sultān Sahāk.  
یا حق.  
یا سلطان سهاک.

Pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā.  
پاکی، راستی، نیستی، رضا.

Har che hast az Ḥaqq ast,  
har che mī-khāhīm be Ḥaqq mī-sepārīm:  
dānāyī-ye sudmand, zehn-e rowshan, dil-e ārām,  
bakht-e nīk dar emtehān,  
va pīshraft-e pāk dar ʿelm,  
bī-āzārī be khalq, bī-kibrī dar del,  
va bī-tajāvuz be haqq-e hīch kas.

Dar ḥadd-e yād-e āshkār mīmānīm,  
be rāh-e Yārī adab mī-dārīm,  
va har niyyat rā be Ḥaqq vā-mīgozārīm.

Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق، یا حق، یا حق.

---

## 雅兹迪信仰

Bi navê Xwedêyê mezin û dilovan.

Şehda dînê min:  
Ez şehdê dînê xwe dikim.  
Xwedê yek e.  
Tawisê Melek heq e.  
Şêx Adî şîrê Xwedê ye.  
Siltan Êzîd padşahê min e.

Sebeha:  
Subhanê Xwedê.  
Subhanê Tawisê Melek.  
Subhanê Şêx Adî.  
Subhanê Êzîdê Sor.

Ya Xwedê,  
di rêya xwendin û fêrbûnê de rêya rast veke.  
Zanîn, bîra zelal, hişê aram û dilê sabir bide.  
Di dersan de ronahî, di nivîsandinê de rastî, di azmûnan de serkeftin û xêr binivîse.  
Çav ji şaşiyê biparêze, dil ji tirsê sivik bike, fikir ji tevliheviyê paqij bike.  
Serkeftin ne bi ziyana kesekî din be, ne bi standina xêr û bereketa kesan be; tenê bi rehma te û rêya rast be.

Ya Xwedê,  
Tawisê Melek bi destûra te li ser rêya xêrê biparêze.  
Şêx Adî bi şîreta pîroz dilê me ber bi rastiyê ve bigire.  
Her gavê xwendinê bibe gavê zanînê, her gotin bibe gotina rast, her kar bibe karê pêşketinê.

Qebûl be li ber dergehê Xwedê.  
Em rêzê ji Şêx, Pîr û Qewwal re digirin; tiştên pîroz û rêûresmên wan bi rûmet bimînin.  
Me di nav dilpakî, paqijî û rêya rast de bihêle.  
Amîn.

---

## 人智学 · 基督社区

In stiller Sammlung richte sich die Seele vor Gott.

Im Namen des Vaters und des Sohnes und des Heiligen Geistes. Amen.

Vor Gott, dem Vater,  
durch Christus Jesus,  
im Licht des Heiligen Geistes,  
bringen wir das Anliegen des Lernens und Erkennens dar.

Christus, Licht der Welt,  
erhelle das Denken,  
reinige das Wollen,  
stärke das Gedächtnis  
und führe das Herz zur Wahrheit.

Für Weisheit im Studium,  
für klare Gedanken,  
für wache Aufmerksamkeit,  
für rechte Prüfungskraft  
und für treuen Fortschritt in der Arbeit  
legen wir dieses Anliegen nicht als Zwang,  
sondern als Opfer des Herzens vor den Christus.

Möge Erfolg nicht auf Kosten anderer gesucht werden,  
nicht durch Neid, Täuschung oder Entzug fremder Möglichkeiten,  
sondern in Wahrheit, Freiheit und Liebe vor Gott.

Vater unser im Himmel,  
geheiligt werde dein Name.  
Dein Reich komme.  
Dein Wille geschehe,  
wie im Himmel, so auf Erden.  
Unser tägliches Brot gib uns heute.  
Und vergib uns unsere Schuld,  
wie auch wir vergeben unsern Schuldigern.  
Und führe uns nicht in Versuchung,  
sondern erlöse uns von dem Bösen.  
Denn dein ist das Reich  
und die Kraft  
und die Herrlichkeit  
in Ewigkeit.  
Amen.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.  
Amen.

Nicht mein Wille,  
sondern dein Wille geschehe.

Was im Lernen zerstreut ist,  
werde vor Christus gesammelt.  
Was im Denken dunkel ist,  
werde durch Wahrheit erhellt.  
Was im Herzen unruhig ist,  
werde durch Frieden geordnet.  
Was im Erfolg ungeordnet begehrt wird,  
werde nicht durch Zwang,  
sondern durch Freiheit, Gewissen und Liebe vor Gott verwandelt.

Im Frieden Christi.  
Amen.

---

## Aurum Solis

In stillness and in purity I stand within the Light of the Ogdoadic Star.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός,  
Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός,  
Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος,  
ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.

Let the work be established in the matter of wisdom, lucid mind, fortunate examination, and steady advancement in study.

ΙΑΩ.  
Ἀγαθὸς Δαίμων.  
ΙΑΩ.

Holy and deathless Light, source and crown of the work, receive this vow:  
I seek increase of learning, clarity of thought, right memory, disciplined attention, and progress in all lawful studies, without falsehood, without malice, without dispossessing another, and without violation of the rightful will of any soul.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός,  
Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός,  
Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος,  
ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Let the noetic light illumine study, reading, examination, judgment, recollection, and expression:

Ἀγαθὸς Δαίμων.  
ΙΑΩ.

May the mind be made clear as the solar heaven;  
may memory be ordered in harmony;  
may diligence be strengthened by virtue;  
may confusion, fear, and dullness be dissolved into rightful measure;  
may examinations and academic undertakings proceed in clarity, justice, and right timing.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.  
ΙΑΩ. ΙΑΩ. ΙΑΩ.

The word is spoken, the measure is sealed, and the force is returned to its proper sphere.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός,  
Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός,  
Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος,  
ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Let every undue compulsion cease; let personal desire be withdrawn into silence; let all powers invoked return peacefully to their own stations.  
By purity, by the sacred word, and by the ordered Light, let the wards be closed in harmony.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.

Fiat. Amen.

## BOTA

In the One Life, centered in stillness, I stand in reverence before the Light.

Holy art Thou, Lord of the Universe.  
Holy art Thou, Whom Nature hath not formed.  
Holy art Thou, the Vast and the Mighty One.  
Lord of the Light and of the Darkness.

אהיה  
Ehyeh.

יה  
Yah.

יהוה אלהים  
YHVH Elohim.

Before the One Life, I set forth this aspiration: may wisdom increase in study and reading; may the mind be clear, steady, and receptive; may examinations and academic occasions unfold in right order; may learning advance with diligence, humility, and true understanding.

Let every word concerning this aspiration be ordered by Wisdom, measured by Understanding, balanced by Beauty, and grounded in righteous manifestation.  
Let this prayer bind no will, coerce no person, diminish no mind, and take no blessing, merit, opportunity, or success from another.  
Let obstacles be clarified and removed without harm, and let all attainment serve the true good of all concerned.

א  
Aleph: let the Breath of the One Life move silently through thought, making the mind lucid and awake.

ב  
Beth: let the house of study be inwardly ordered, that memory, attention, and comprehension may dwell together in peace.

ג  
Gimel: let the path between understanding and expression be made clear, so that what is learned may be rightly recalled and rightly spoken.

אהיה יה יהוה אלהים  
Ehyeh. Yah. YHVH Elohim.

May Wisdom shine above, Understanding give form within, and the clear Light of the One Life guide study, reading, memory, discernment, and right action.

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
ve-Geburah.  
ve-Gedulah.  
le-Olam.  
Amen.

May every motive be purified in the Light; may every desire for knowledge be freed from vanity, fear, domination, and confusion.  
May the fruits of learning be dedicated to truth, service, and the harmony of the One Life.

Holy art Thou, Lord of the Universe.  
Holy art Thou, Whom Nature hath not formed.  
Holy art Thou, the Vast and the Mighty One.  
Lord of the Light and of the Darkness.

Amen.

---

## 祆教 / 琐罗亚斯德教

### —— Padyab 洁净立界 ——
Pa nām i yazdān, Ohrmazd Khodāe awazūnī.  
Humata, hukhta, hvarshta andar Asha.

### —— Khshnaothra ——
Khshnaothra Ahurahe Mazdāo.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— Niyyat / Dibache ——
为求学读书智慧增长、心思清明、考运亨通、学业精进；唯愿在 Asha 中成就善思、善言、善行，不夺他人福分，不损他人寿数，不以胜利求他人败坏。

Pa nām i yazdān, Ohrmazd Khodāe awazūnī.  
Humata hukhta hvarshta andar Asha.

### —— Kem Na Mazda / Kusti 守护 ——
Kêm-nâ mazdâ mavaitê pâyûm dadå,  
hyat mâ dregvå dîdareshatâ aênanghê,  
anyêm thwahmât âthrascâ mananghascâ,  
ýayå shyaothanâish ashem thraoshtâ ahurâ,  
tãm môi dãstvãm daênayâi frâvaocâ.  

Kê verethrem-jâ thwâ pôi sêñghâ ýôi heñtî,  
cithrâ môi dãm ahûmbish ratûm cizhdî,  
at hôi vohû seraoshô jañtû mananghâ,  
mazdâ ahmâi ýahmâi vashî kahmâicît.  

Pâta-nô tbishyañtat pairi mazdåsca ârmaitishca speñtasca,  
nase daêvî druxsh, nase daêvô-cithre, nase daêvô-frakarshte, nase daêvô-fradâiti,  
apa druxsh nase, apa druxsh dvâra, apa druxsh vînase, apâxedhre apa-nasyehe,  
mâ mereñcainîsh gaêthå astvaitîsh ashahe,  
nemascâ ýâ ârmaitish îzhâcâ.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— Ahura Mazda Khodāe / Patet 悔净 ——
Ahura-Mazda khodāe, Ahereman awā-dashãn, dur avāz dāshtār, zad shekasteh bād.  

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum,  
az harvastīn dushmata duzhukhta duzhvarshta,  
mem pa getī manīd, oem goft, oem kard, oem jast, oem būn būd ested.  

Az ān gunāh, manashnī gavashnī kunashnī, tanī ravānī getī minōānī,  
okhe awākhsh pashemān, pa se gavashnī pa patet hom.

### —— Jasa me Avanghe Mazda / Fravarane ——
Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda.  

Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē āstūtascā fravaretascā.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Āstuyē daēnām vanguhīm Māzdayasnīm,  
fraspāyaokhedhrām, nidhāsnaithishem, khvaētvadathām ashaonīm,  
yā hāitināmchā būshyeintināmchā mazishtāchā vahishtāchā sraēshtāchā,  
yā āhūirish Zarathushtrish.  
Ahurāi Mazdāi vīspā vohū chinahmī.  
Aēshā astī daēnayāo Māzdayasnōish āstūitish.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 核心 manthra ——
Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

Yenghē hātām āat yesnē paiti vanghō,  
Mazdāo Ahurō vaēthā ashāt hachā,  
yāonghāmchā tāschā tāschā yazamaidē.

### —— 正行：Daena / Gatha Orientation ——
Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Daênãm vanguhîm Māzdayasnîm yazamaide.  
Manthrem Spentem yazamaide.

Humata andar Asha; hukhta andar Asha; hvarshta andar Asha.  
Daênā vanguhī, vohū mananghō, xratūm, sraoshem, ashem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— Ahmai Raeshcha / Doa Tan-Dorosti 祝祷 ——
Ahmāi raēshcha khvarenanghacha,  
Ahmāi tanvō drvatātem,  
Ahmāi tanvō vazdvārē,  
Ahmāi tanvō verethrem,  
Ahmāi ishtim pourush-khathrem,  
Ahmāi asnāmchit frazantim,  
Ahmāi darekham darekho-jītim,  
Ahmāi vahishtem ahum ashaonām,  
raochanghem vispō-khathrem.

Tandarosti, dorosti, zor, niru, khoreh, awazuni,  
ravāni shād, tan dorost, geti minōānī andar Asha.  

Ahmāi raēshcha; Hazanghrem; Jasa me Avanghe Mazda; Kerfeh Mozd.

### —— 回结悔净护持 ——
Az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

## A∴A∴

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

I stand within the current of A∴A∴ and set my will toward the Knowledge and Conversation of the Holy Guardian Angel: not for vanity, coercion, or the disturbance of another will, but according to the True Will.

愿求学读书智慧增长，心思清明，考运亨通，学业精进；不夺他人福分，不损他人道路，不以此愿操纵他人意志，唯愿一切所成合于真意志与正当功课。

A ka dua  
Tuf ur biu  
Bi a’a chefu  
Dudu ner af an nuteru.

In the Name of the Most High, and under the oath of the Great Work, I banish from this place all confusion, obsession, falsehood, sloth, fear, and wandering force that is not in accord with the Work.

Ateh.

## 混沌魔法（Chaos Magick）

I banish from this working all obsession, confusion, reflected desire, and lust of result.

Neither-neither.  
I am not this.  
I am not that.  
No belief is true.  
Everything is permitted.

KIA.  
ZOS.  
KIA.  
ZOS.

This is my will:  
Study-wisdom increases; the mind is clear; memory is ordered; insight arises swiftly; examinations open by right chance; learning advances steadily.

This working takes nothing by theft, diminishes no other mind, fortune, or life.

The sign is made:  
THE SIGIL OF CLEAR STUDY.

The desire is bound into the sign.  
The sign is empty of words.  
The sign is full of will.

IAŌ.  
SABAŌ.  
ABRASAX.  
ZAZAS ZAZAS NASATANADA ZAZAS.  
IAŌ SABAŌ ABRASAX.

By gnosis, by silence, by the death of thought:  
THE SIGIL OF CLEAR STUDY is launched.

It is done.  
It is forgotten.  
It is no longer mine.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

I banish again all residue, obsession, and borrowed masks.  
The sign is released into silence; attachment is cut; the ordinary self returns.  
Feet to earth, breath to body, mind to the present.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

The working is closed.  
The mask is removed.  
The record remains: one neutral mark, without desire.

## 现代术士派（Cochranian、Sabbatic Craft）

In the name of the Old One,  
Master of the Crooked Path,  
Keeper of the hidden fire,  
I hallow this compass.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
let this ring be whole,  
let no false word enter,  
let no oath be broken,  
let no secret be profaned.

Old One, hear this word.  
The work is for wisdom:  
for increase of learning, clearness of mind, steadiness in study, right memory in the hour of trial, good fortune in examination, and true progress in all honest scholarship.

No stolen oath is spoken here.  
No hidden word is claimed here.  
Only the open charm is set,  
only the rightful prayer is made.

Fire in the head, light in the bone,  
the crooked road beneath the feet;  
let cunning be awakened,  
let folly be uncovered,  
let the true sign be known.

Let the eye be clear upon the page,  
let the ear be keen to the teacher’s word,  
let the hand be steady in its writing,  
let memory hold what is needful,  
let fear be cooled,  
let wandering thought be gathered,  
let diligence ripen into skill.

Let success come by rightful road,  
not by theft of another’s portion,  
not by dimming another’s lamp,  
not by breaking another’s chance,  
but by honest labour, clear wit, and fitting grace.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
the word is spoken,  
the work is sealed,  
the compass is whole.

If any word has gone beyond its rightful bound,  
let it be withdrawn and made harmless.  
If any door has been opened amiss,  
let it be shut in peace.  
If any edge has been set too keen,  
let it be turned aside from harm.

Old One, receive thanks.  
Let the road be shut where it must be shut.  
Let the road be open where it must be open.  
Peace to the ring,  
peace to the dead,  
peace to the living.

So mote it be.

---

## 共济会

Most holy and glorious Lord God,  
the Great Architect of the Universe,  
the Giver of all good gifts and graces:

Thou hast promised that where two or three are gathered together in Thy Name,  
Thou wilt be in the midst of them and bless them.

In Thy Name, and in reverence before Thy presence,  
we place this petition concerning the increase of wisdom in study,  
clearness of mind in reading and learning,  
upright success in examinations,  
and steady advancement in all worthy scholarship.

Grant that every thought, word, and act  
may be ordered by Wisdom,  
supported by Strength,  
and adorned with Beauty.  
Let the mind be as a well-laid stone,  
true to the line, square in intention,  
and fit for the building of a virtuous life.

הִנֵּה מַה־טּוֹב וּמַה־נָּעִים  
שֶׁבֶת אַחִים גַּם־יָחַד׃

Let Brotherly Love, Relief, and Truth  
govern our hearts toward all brethren and all mankind.  
Let no envy, vanity, unlawful gain, false witness,  
or betrayal of trust enter this labor.  
In seeking success, we do not seek to dispossess another,  
to darken another’s light,  
or to take from another’s rightful opportunity.

Direct the studies now undertaken;  
open the understanding to receive what is true,  
strengthen memory without confusion,  
steady the hand and heart in examination,  
and make diligence fruitful in due season.  
May learning become not pride, but service;  
not idle display, but moral improvement;  
not selfish advantage, but a lamp set in order.

Keep us faithful to every lawful obligation,  
silent where silence is due,  
truthful where speech is required,  
temperate in desire,  
upright in conduct,  
and charitable toward all mankind.

May the Supreme Grand Master  
preside over this intention,  
until all work is closed in peace.

So mote it be.

---

## 玫瑰十字 Lectorium Rosicrucianum

静默。

在此承认自身真实意向：  
愿求学读书智慧增长，心思清明，考运亨通，学业精进。  
愿此意向不为强制，不为贪求，不为支配，不为伤害；不夺他人福分，不损他人道路。  
愿一切偏离真实光明之念，在静默中止息。

Κύριε τοῦ Φωτός,  
ὁ νοῦς καθαρθήτω,  
ἡ διάνοια φωτισθήτω,  
ἡ μνήμη εὐτακτήτω,  
ὁ λόγος ἀληθευέτω,  
καὶ ἡ σπουδὴ γινέσθω ἐν πραΰτητι καὶ σωφροσύνῃ.

Ἐν ἀρχῇ ἦν ὁ Λόγος,  
καὶ ὁ Λόγος ἦν πρὸς τὸν Θεόν,  
καὶ Θεὸς ἦν ὁ Λόγος.  
οὗτος ἦν ἐν ἀρχῇ πρὸς τὸν Θεόν.  
πάντα δι’ αὐτοῦ ἐγένετο,  
καὶ χωρὶς αὐτοῦ ἐγένετο οὐδὲ ἕν.  
ὃ γέγονεν ἐν αὐτῷ ζωὴ ἦν,  
καὶ �

## 东方圣殿骑士团（OTO）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

I set forth my will in this prayer:  
that wisdom may increase in study and reading; that the mind be clear, steady, and luminous; that examinations and trials of learning be met with right order, courage, and fortunate passage; and that scholarship advance according to True Will.  
I seek no theft of another star’s light, no diminution of another’s way, but only the right unfolding of knowledge, discipline, memory, and understanding.

I believe in one secret and ineffable LORD; and in one Star in the Company of Stars of whose fire we are created, and to which we shall return; and in one Father of Life, Mystery of Mystery, in His name CHAOS, the sole viceregent of the Sun upon the Earth; and in one Air the nourisher of all that breathes.

A ka dua  
Tuf ur biu  
Bi a'a chefu  
Dudu ner af an nuteru.

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:  
I, I adore thee!

Every man and every woman is a star.  
The word of the Law is Θελημα.  
Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

Let the lamp of Will be kindled in the intellect;  
let confusion be banished from the chamber of thought;  
let memory stand firm, attention be gathered, and judgment be balanced.  
In Light, Life, Love, and Liberty, may study become a path of awakening,  
and may every page, question, and examination be ordered under Will.

There is no part of me that is not of the gods.

APO PANTOS KAKODAIMONOS.  
IO PAN, IO PAN PAN.  
IO ISCHUROS, IO ATHANATOS, IO ABROTOS, IO IAO.  
HAGIOS, HAGIOS, HAGIOS IAO.

Love is the law, love under will.

## 赫密士主义当代社团

[净化与定向]  
In silentio, pietate et mente clara sto; non ad nocendum, non ad cogendum, non ad fallendum, non ad rapiendum oro.  
Sit haec oratio sub ordine sacro: τὸ ἕν, νοῦς, λόγος.

[向一者与Nous发愿]  
Ad τὸ ἕν me converto; ad νοῦς mentem attollo; per λόγος verba mea temperentur.  
Fiat in me puritas intentionis, modestia studii, et amor verae cognitionis.

[神圣呼语：Corpus Hermeticum XIII, Secret Hymn]  
Hagios ho Theos, ho Patēr tōn holōn.  
Hagios ho Theos, hou hē boulē teleitai tais idiais dynameisin.  
Hagios ho Theos, hos gnōsthēnai bouletai kai ginōsketai tois idiois.

Hagios ei, ho logō systēsas ta onta.  
Hagios ei, hou pasa physis eikōn ephu.  
Hagios ei, hon hē physis ouk emorphōsen.  
Hagios ei, ho pasēs dynameōs ischyroteros.  
Hagios ei, ho pantos hyperechōn.  
Hagios ei, ho kreittōn epainou.

[陈明所愿]  
愿求学读书之智慧增长，心思清明，考运亨通，学业精进；愿记忆有序，理解明彻，临考安定，笔下不乱。愿此成就不夺他人福分，不损他人机会，不以欺诈取胜，不以骄慢炫耀知识；但愿一切进益皆归于敬虔、节制、真知与正当努力。

[赫密士感恩祷：Asclepius 41]  
Tibi gratias agimus, summe et excellentissime,  
cuius numine solo gubernamur;  
et gratias agimus tibi, qui nos tanto lumine cognitionis inlustrasti.

Sanctum est nomen tuum et honorabile,  
nomen unum, quo solus Deus benedicendus est religione paterna,  
quoniam omnibus paternam pietatem, religionem, amorem  
et quaecumque sunt dulcioris affectus praestare dignatus es.

[感恩]  
Non impero sacro; sed supplex oro, audio, et corrigor.  
Gratias ago pro lumine cognitionis, pro ordine mentis, pro disciplina studii, pro pace cordis.

[回向与静默]  
Quod clarum est, purificetur; quod inquietum est, quiescat; quod superbum est, humilietur; quod utile est, ad bonum convertatur.  
Sit omnis fructus huius orationis in sapientia, temperantia, veritate et pace.  
In silentio dimitto cupiditatem, metum et perturbationem; in gratiarum actione redeo ad ordinem sacrum.

Sigē. Nous. Logos. Hen.

---

## 玛丁主义（Martinism）

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Seigneur, Dieu éternel, source de toute lumière, de toute justice et de toute miséricorde,  
que notre pensée, notre parole et notre acte soient redressés devant Toi.  
Seigneur Jésus-Christ, Réparateur,  
que ta paix descende sur l’intention droite ici présentée :  
ut studium augeatur, mens purificetur, sapientia crescat, memoria ordinetur,  
et via scholarum sub tua luce procedat.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Et secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum, dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Redde mihi laetitiam salutaris tui,  
et spiritu principali confirma me.

Asperges me, Domine, hyssopo, et mundabor;  
lavabis me, et super nivem dealbabor.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt:  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum:  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Lux Verbi divini illuminet intellectum;  
pax Réparateuris componat cor;  
ordo Spiritus Sancti dirigat memoriam, attentionem et judicium.  
Non petimus gloriam vanam, nec aliorum bonum auferre,  
nec lucem proximi minuere;  
sed petimus humiliter sapientiam, claritatem mentis, constantiam studii,  
rectam occasionem in examine, et fructum laboris honesti.  
Fiat voluntas tua.

Seigneur, que l’intérieur temple soit purifié du trouble,  
que la dispersion retourne au silence,  
que l’ardeur d’apprendre soit unie à la charité,  
et que toute science serve la vérité, la justice et la paix.  
Per Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Ne proicias me a facie tua,  
et Spiritum sanctum tuum ne auferas a me.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

## Reclaiming（Starhawk）

Ground of being, Earth below and within,  
I center in breath, body, and presence.  
I come into my body.  
I come into this moment.  
I come into the turning spiral of learning.

By my will, by my breath, by my truth,  
this circle is cast:  
a boundary of clarity, consent, and love,  
a place of power-with, not power-over.

East, powers of Air:  
breath, song, thought, and dawn,  
be present in this circle.  
Clear the mind; sharpen attention; open the path of study.

South, powers of Fire:  
will, courage, heat, and transformation,  
be present in this circle.  
Strengthen discipline, confidence, and steady effort.

West, powers of Water:  
feeling, dream, grief, and healing,  
be present in this circle.  
Calm anxiety; soothe fear; let memory flow cleanly.

North, powers of Earth:  
body, root, stone, and bread,  
be present in this circle.  
Ground knowledge in practice; make learning strong and lasting.

Goddess, immanent one,  
She who is within and around all beings,  
be present in this circle.  
Ancient One of the spiral,  
bright in the mind, deep in the body,  
hold this work in wisdom and love.

Air I am,  
Fire I am,  
Water, Earth, and Spirit I am.

For the growth of wisdom,  
for a clear mind in reading and study,  
for good fortune in examinations,  
for steady progress in learning,  
I raise this prayer.

Let this blessing come without dispossessing another,  
without stealing another’s chance,  
without diminishing another’s path.  
Let success arise through clarity, preparation, fairness,  
right timing, and the shared good.

Let love, law, knowledge, liberty, and wisdom  
stand as five bright points within the heart.  
Let love keep learning humane.  
Let law give order and method.  
Let knowledge be remembered and understood.  
Let liberty free the mind from fear.  
Let wisdom guide every answer, choice, and word.

She changes everything She touches,  
and everything She touches changes.

Let confusion be changed into insight.  
Let scattered thought be changed into focus.  
Let fear of failure be changed into courage.  
Let dullness be changed into living curiosity.  
Let effort become skill,  
and skill become confidence,  
and confidence become clear action.

May the pages open.  
May the mind be bright.  
May memory be faithful.  
May questions be understood.  
May answers come in order.  
May the hand be steady,  
the breath be calm,  
the heart be brave,  
and the work be blessed.

Earth my body,  
Water my blood,  
Air my breath,  
and Fire my spirit.

The power is raised.  
The power is released.  
The power is grounded in Earth,  
carried by Water,  
quickened by Air,  
tempered by Fire,  
and returned to Spirit.

Goddess, immanent one,  
for presence and witness, blessed be.

North, powers of Earth,  
for body and ground, blessed be.

West, powers of Water,  
for feeling and healing, blessed be.

South, powers of Fire,  
for will and transformation, blessed be.

East, powers of Air,  
for breath and song, blessed be.

The circle is open, but unbroken.  
May the peace of the Goddess be ever in the heart.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

All power raised here is now released and grounded.  
All coercive intent is undone.  
All fear is named and given back to Earth to be composted.  
Consent is restored; freedom is honored; power-with remains.  
Where harm has been done, may repair become possible.  
May this work return as blessing to all beings,  
to the land, the waters, the air, the fire,  
and the living web that holds us all. Blessed be.

---

## Spiritism · Kardecism（凯德克派）

Dieu tout-puissant, souverainement juste et bon,  
que ta volonté soit faite et non la nôtre.  
Si la demande que nous formons est utile à notre âme,  
si elle sert notre progrès moral, notre intelligence droite et notre devoir,  
et si elle est conforme à ta loi, daigne l’accueillir.

Notre Père qui êtes aux cieux,  
que votre nom soit sanctifié;  
que votre règne arrive;  
que votre volonté soit faite sur la terre comme au ciel.  
Donnez-nous aujourd’hui notre pain de chaque jour;  
pardonnez-nous nos offenses,  
comme nous pardonnons à ceux qui nous ont offensés;  
ne nous laissez pas succomber à la tentation,  
mais délivrez-nous du mal.  
Ainsi soit-il.

Bons Esprits qui êtes les ministres de Dieu,  
assistez-nous dans l’épreuve présente.  
Anges gardiens, Esprits protecteurs,  
éclairez notre pensée, soutenez notre courage,  
écartez de nous les pensées mauvaises,  
la paresse, la vanité, la peur et la confusion,  
et inspirez-nous ce qui est juste, charitable, humble  
et conforme à la loi de Dieu.

Seigneur,  
nous te prions pour l’étude, la lecture, l’examen et le progrès dans l’instruction.  
Accorde-nous une pensée claire, une mémoire fidèle,  
un jugement calme, une attention persévérante,  
et le goût sincère d’apprendre afin de mieux servir et mieux nous améliorer.  
Que la réussite demandée ne soit point recherchée par orgueil, fraude, injustice,  
ni au détriment d’autrui;  
qu’elle ne ravisse à personne son bien, sa place légitime, sa paix ou son mérite.  
Qu’elle soit le fruit du travail honnête, de la patience,  
de la discipline et de l’inspiration des bons Esprits.

Mon Dieu, inspirez-nous la meilleure résolution  
dans nos études et dans les épreuves scolaires.  
Bons Esprits qui nous protégez,  
aidez-nous à discerner ce qui est conforme à la charité,  
à la justice et à l’humilité.  
Faites que nous sachions employer l’intelligence reçue  
non pour dominer, mais pour comprendre;  
non pour nous glorifier, mais pour progresser;  
non pour tromper, mais pour accomplir notre devoir.

Nous prions aussi pour tous ceux qui étudient, enseignent, examinent,  
ou portent l’inquiétude de l’avenir;  
que les vivants soient soutenus dans leurs efforts,  
que les âmes souffrantes reçoivent la lumière et la paix,  
et que toute pensée de jalousie, de découragement ou de rivalité amère  
soit remplacée par la bienveillance et le courage.

Seigneur,  
ne permets pas que cette prière serve l’orgueil,  
l’intérêt égoïste, la curiosité frivole,  
ni la domination d’aucune créature visible ou invisible.  
Aide-nous à corriger nos défauts,  
à réparer nos négligences,  
à pardonner avec sincérité,  
à demander pardon lorsque nous avons manqué à la charité,  
et à faire de chaque connaissance acquise  
un moyen de devenir meilleurs.

Que cette prière soit seulement un acte de foi,  
de charité, de repentir et de soumission à ta volonté.  
À Dieu seul appartiennent la sagesse, la justice et la bonté.  
Ainsi soit-il.

---

## 神智学协会

In the name of the One Life, and for the good of the whole human family, this prayer is held for the increase of wisdom in study and reading, for clarity of mind, favorable conditions in examinations, and steady progress in learning, within right human relations and the Plan of Love and Light.

From the point of Light within the Mind of God  
Let light stream forth into the minds of men.  
Let Light descend on Earth.

May the light of discernment illumine thought, memory, attention, and understanding; may study be sincere, orderly, and fruitful.

From the point of Love within the Heart of God  
Let love stream forth into the hearts of men.  
May Christ return to Earth.

May learning be joined to goodwill, humility, patience, and service; may success not be sought by depriving others, diminishing others, or bending any will.

From the centre where the Will of God is known  
Let purpose guide the little wills of men—  
The purpose which the Masters know and serve.

May purpose guide the will to diligence, right effort, clear judgment, and calm courage in examinations and all works of learning.

From the centre which we call the race of men  
Let the Plan of Love and Light work out  
And may it seal the door where evil dwells.

May confusion, fear, harmful influence, and selfish misuse be sealed away; may obstacles be removed without harm, retaliation, or coercion.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.

May this aspiration be purified of separateness and held only within Light, Love, Power, and the good of humanity; may wisdom gained be used for service, right human relations, and the blessing of all beings.

---

## Spiritualism / NSAC

Infinite Intelligence, God of love, law, and life,  
I come in reverence, in sincerity, and in personal responsibility,  
holding the desire for growing wisdom, clear thought, favorable examination conditions, and steady academic progress before Thee.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

I affirm:  
We believe in Infinite Intelligence.  
We believe that the phenomena of Nature, both physical and spiritual,  
are the expression of Infinite Intelligence.  
We affirm that true religion is living in obedience to Nature's Laws.  
We affirm that the existence and personal identity of the individual  
continue after the change called death.  
We affirm that communication with the so-called dead is a fact,  
scientifically proven by the phenomena of Spiritualism.  
We affirm the highest morality contained in the Golden Rule:  
Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you,  
do ye even so to them.  
We affirm moral responsibility, and that each soul makes its own happiness  
or unhappiness as it obeys or disobeys Nature's physical and spiritual laws.  
We affirm that the doorway to reformation is never closed  
against any soul here or hereafter.  
We affirm that the precepts of Prophecy and Healing are Divine attributes  
proven through Mediumship.

Infinite Intelligence,  
within Divine Law, truth, compassion, and the welfare of all concerned,  
let the mind be made clear, steady, and receptive to right understanding.  
Let study be disciplined, memory orderly, speech truthful, and judgment sound.  
Let confusion, fear, distraction, and discouragement be gently removed,  
and let diligence, patience, and moral courage increase day by day.  
In examinations and all tests of learning, let there be calm attention, fair opportunity,  
right timing, and the ability to express honestly what has been learned.  
May academic progress come through effort, integrity, and obedience to Nature’s Laws,  
not through deceit, coercion, or harm to any other soul.  
I seek no success that deprives another of rightful good,  
and no advantage that would lessen another’s honest path.

Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart,  
be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.

May no word spoken here replace conscience, responsibility, study, or truth.  
May no spirit, person, or influence be compelled.  
May all be governed by Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law.

I release all anxious seeking after signs, messages, or certainty,  
and return to quiet prayer, honest labor, and personal responsibility.  
In silence, may the heart rest under Divine Law.  
Where practical help is needed, may there be willingness to seek wise teachers, proper counsel, and fitting professional care.  
May light, peace, and right understanding remain.

Amen.

---

## 瑟勒玛（Thelema）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

Under the Law of Thelema, in the matter of study, reading, wisdom, clear mind, good examination fortune, and advancement in learning, let this word be set in harmony with True Will.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.

ΣΟΙ, Ὦ ΦΑΛΛΕ, ἸΣΧΥΡΟΣ, ΕΥΧΑΡΙΣΤΟΣ, ΙΑΩ.

ΘΗΡΙΟΝ.

ΝΥΙΤ.

ΒΑΒΑΛΟΝ.

ΑΔΙΤ.

ΙΩ ΠΑΝ.

ΠΡΟ ΜΟΥ ΙΥΓΓΕΣ,  
ΟΠΙΣΩ ΜΟΥ ΤΕΛΕΤΑΡΧΑΙ,  
ΕΠΙ ΔΕΞΙΑ ΣΥΝΟΧΕΣ,  
ΕΠΑΡΙΣΤΕΡΑ ΔΑΙΜΟΝΕΣ,  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun. Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm. Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Night!

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:—  
I, I adore thee!

Appear on the throne of Ra!  
Open the ways of the Khu!  
Lighten the ways of the Ka!  
The ways of the Khabs run through  
To stir me or still me!  
Aum! let it fill me!

Let there be increase of wisdom, clarity of thought, right memory, steady attention, fortunate passage through examinations, and continual progress in study; let the Knowledge and Conversation of the Holy Guardian Angel illumine the path of learning and discernment.

愿求学读书智慧增长，心思清明，考运亨通，学业精进；不夺他人之光，不损他人之路，不以一星限制另一星，惟令所愿安置于 True Will 之中。

Let this petition be ordered according to True Will, without restriction of another star, without coercion, and without harm.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.

ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Love is the law, love under will.

---

## 威卡 Alexandrian

I stand within the Circle, in perfect love and perfect trust.  
Let all within this rite be bounded by the Rede:  
An it harm none, do what ye will.

By Air, by Fire, by Water, by Earth,  
this Circle is cast and sealed.  
Between the worlds, and in the presence of the Mighty Ones,  
let this rite be held for the increase of wisdom, clear mind, fortunate examinations, and steady progress in study.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

O Goddess,  
Great Mother, Lady of the Moon,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother.  
Kindle inner wisdom, calm the wandering mind,  
and let understanding ripen in study, reading, memory, and judgment.

O God,  
Lord of the Greenwood, Horned One,  
guardian of life, death, and return,  
Strengthen discipline, courage, and right effort,  
that learning may be pursued with steadiness and honor.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For wisdom in learning,  
for clarity of thought,  
for good fortune in examinations,  
for diligence, comprehension, and academic progress,  
within right will, right boundary, and harm to none,  
let the prayer be shaped in truth.

May success come without theft of another’s chance,  
without dimming another’s mind,  
without dispossessing any soul of rightful blessing.  
May obstacles be cleared, not by harm, but by light, order, patience, and skill.

So mote it be.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

The Circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.

Blessed be.

All that is unsettled is now grounded.  
All excess is released into Earth, to be made clean and harmless.  
By the Rede I reaffirm: An it harm none, do what ye will.  
In clear boundary, in peaceful will, and in perfect trust, this rite is ended.

---

## 威卡 Dianic

By earth and moon, by breath and flame,  
this place is made sacred.

I cast this circle as a boundary of truth,  
a circle of protection,  
a circle of blessing,  
a circle of the Goddess.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
Mother of the wild places,  
Keeper of women’s mysteries,  
be present in this circle.

I stand before you in sincerity.  
I name the matter of this rite:  
may wisdom increase in study and learning;  
may the mind be clear, steady, and bright;  
may examinations unfold with right fortune;  
may scholarship deepen, discipline strengthen,  
and understanding grow.

Let this prayer touch only what may be touched in freedom.  
Let it bind no unwilling heart.  
Let it cross no oath-bound door.  
Let it harm none.

O Diana,  
look upon this path of study,  
this labor of reading, memory, thought, and discernment.

Where there is confusion, let there be inner knowing.  
Where there is distraction, let there be calm attention.  
Where there is fear, let there be clear boundary.  
Where there is weariness, let there be renewal.  
Where there is pride, let there be humility.  
Where there is effort, let there be growth.

May learning come by honest work.  
May success come without stealing another’s chance,  
without diminishing another’s blessing,  
without bending another’s will.  
May every answer remembered be rightful,  
every insight earned be clean,  
every opportunity opened be harmless and just.

All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.

I place within this circle:  
my breath, my attention, my goodwill,  
and the steady flame of the seeking mind.

By the waxing, full, and waning Moon,  
by the dark and returning Moon,  
may what is true be strengthened,  
may what is harmful be dissolved,  
may what belongs to wisdom return to the mind,  
may what is not needed depart in peace.

For wisdom in learning, clarity in thought, good fortune in examinations,  
and steady progress in study,  
I ask blessing, clarity, and right unfolding.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

O Diana,  
I thank you for your presence.  
Remain if you will,  
depart if you must,  
with blessing between us.

The circle is open,  
but unbroken.  
Merry meet,  
merry part,  
and merry meet again.

May this rite end in freedom, not compulsion;  
in blessing, not control;  
in clean boundaries, not trespass;  
in wisdom that harms none.

---

## Dievturība（拉脱维亚）

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
stāv pie mācīšanās un grāmatu ceļa,  
stāv pie skaidras domas,  
stāv pie gudrības augšanas.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā;  
Dievs, dod man otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt.

Par mācībām, lasīšanu un pārbaudījumiem es saku taisnu vārdu:  
lai mana doma ir skaidra,  
lai mans prāts ir modrs,  
lai mana atmiņa ir stipra,  
lai mans spriedums ir godīgs,  
lai mans darbs ir rūpīgs,  
lai mans ceļš zinībās ir taisns.  

Lai veicas pārbaudījumos pēc darba un tikuma,  
lai gudrība aug bez lepnības,  
lai sekmes nāk bez sveša labuma atņemšanas,  
lai mana roka nedara pāri nevienam.

Dod, Dieviņi, otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt;  
Otram devu, sev palika,  
Savu mūžu dzīvojot.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā.

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
pieņem šo vārdu par skaidru prātu,  
pieņem šo dainu par mācību ceļu.  

Ar tīru dziesmu, ar taisnu darbu, ar labu tikumu  
lai šis vārds paliek mierā un gaismā.  

Lai top.

---

## 巴斯克 Sorginak 复兴

Ni hemen nago.  
Hitz hau nire ahoan, arnasa nire bularrean, lurra nire oinen azpian.

Agur, Mari Anbotoko Dama.  
Agur, Lurraren bihotzeko andrea.  
Entzun nire hitza, entzun nire arnasa.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.

Nire eskaria hau da:  
ikasketetan jakinduria haz dadila,  
irakurtzean eta ikastean gogoa garbi gera dadila,  
oroimena sendo, adimena argi, eta bihotza bare izan dadila.  
Azterketen bidean zorte ona eta zuzentasuna ager daitezela,  
lanak aurrera egin dezala, eta ikasbidea egunero hobetu dadila.

Ez dadila nire arrakasta besteen zortea kenduz etorri.  
Ez dadila nire bidea besteen bidea ilunduz ireki.  
Nire jakinduria egiaz, ahaleginez, eta neurri onez hazi dadila.

Eguzki amandrea, argitu bidea.  
Ilargi amandrea, gorde isila.  
Lurra, hartu nekea.  
Haizea, eraman beldurra.  
Ura, garbitu nahasmena.  
Sua, piztu indarra.

Ez dut kalterik nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Ez dut gezurrik zin egiten.  
Ez dut sorgin izena gaizki erabiltzen.

Mari Anbotoko Dama,  
nire hitza entzuna izan dadila,  
nire muga gordea izan dadila,  
nire bidea argitua izan dadila.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.  
Hala bedi.

---

## 威卡 Eclectic

By earth and sea and sky,  
let this circle be cast and sealed.  
What enters here shall enter in truth;  
what leaves here shall leave in peace.

I stand within the circle between the worlds,  
in perfect love and perfect trust,  
for wisdom, clear mind, good fortune in examinations,  
and steady progress in learning and study.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of wisdom and study.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of wisdom and study.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of wisdom and study.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of wisdom and study.

Great Mother,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother,  
who of old was called Artemis, Astarte, Dione, Melusine,  
Aphrodite, Cerridwen, Diana, Arionrhod, Brigid, and by many other names.  
All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.  
Be present to this prayer for wisdom, study, and clear knowing.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life, death, and return,  
be present to this prayer for discipline, courage, and right effort.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

Therefore I speak only within willing, rightful, and harmless bounds:  
may wisdom increase;  
may the mind be clear, calm, and bright;  
may memory be steady, understanding deepened,  
and learning ripen through honest effort.  
May examination fortune be favorable through preparation, clarity, and right timing.  
May study advance without envy, coercion, deceit, or harm.  
Let no will be bound.  
Let no heart be compelled.  
Let no life be diminished.  
Let no success be taken by dispossessing another,  
and let no blessing be gained by lessening another’s path.  
Let what is not mine return to its own place.  
Let what is mine stand clear in truth.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For wisdom and study,  
may the crooked be made clear,  
may confusion be made harmless,  
may the hidden be known in right measure,  
may the needed path open without coercion.

If any word of this rite has exceeded rightful boundary,  
I withdraw it now.  
If any force has been called beyond consent,  
I release it now.  
If any bond has been made against true will,  
I unmake it now.  
Peace to all beings touched by this prayer.

Great Mother, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Horned One, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

All unrightful force is withdrawn.  
All unconsented bond is released.  
All excess returns to peace and balance.  
The circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.  
So mote it be.

---

## 威卡 Gardnerian

In this place, in this hour, I stand between the worlds,  
with clean hands, clear speech, and a will held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

I conjure thee, O Circle of Power,  
that thou beest a boundary between the world of men and the realms of the Mighty Ones,  
a guardian and a meeting-place for wisdom, study, clear mind, good examination fortune, and steady learning.

Lady of the Moon, Great Mother, Bright One, Queen of the secret place,  
hear the words spoken within this circle.  
Shine upon the inward lamp; open the quiet door of understanding;  
let memory be ordered, thought be clean, and the heart be calm.

Whenever ye have need of anything,  
once in the month, and better it be when the moon is full,  
then shall ye assemble in some desert place,  
or in a forest all together join  
to adore the potent spirit of your queen.

Horned One, Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life and death,  
stand apart in thy own power and witness this working.  
Grant steadiness of will, discipline of hand, courage before trial,  
and the strength to learn without fear.

Before the Lady I speak the need:  
May study become fruitful; may wisdom increase; may the mind be clear;  
may examinations be met with calm breath, true recall, and right judgment;  
may learning advance by honest effort, patient attention, and living insight.

Before the Lord I speak the boundary:  
Let this prayer harm none, bind none, and bend no will against its truth.  
Let no success be taken by theft of another’s blessing,  
no gain be won by another’s loss,  
and no fear, envy, falsehood, or ill-wrought force have power here.

Let this prayer be for wisdom rightly sought,  
harming none, binding none against the true will,  
and turning aside all confusion, panic, negligence, and self-doubt.

Eko, Eko, Azarak,  
Eko, Eko, Zomelak.

By earth, let learning take lawful root.  
By air, let thought be known in clarity.  
By fire, let diligence be quickened without harm.  
By water, let memory flow in peace.

Lady of the Moon, receive this prayer.  
Horned One, witness this prayer.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, keep it within right measure.

As the cup and the bread are blessed in fellowship,  
so may the work be whole:  
for wisdom, clear study, fair examination fortune, and steady progress,  
according to freedom, honesty, and goodwill toward all.

What is hidden, let it remain veiled;  
what is public and pure, let it bless without overreach.  
What is restless, be cleansed; what is harmful, be turned aside;  
what is rightful, be strengthened in peace.

Lady of the Moon, I thank thee.  
Horned One, I thank thee.  
Mighty Ones, I thank you.  
May this blessing go forth only as love, clarity, courage, and wisdom.

The circle is open, yet unbroken.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

---

## Finnish Suomenusko

Alku aina, alku aina,  
sana synty, virsi nousi.

Minä sanaton sanan etsijä,  
lausun sanat hiljaisessa mielessä,  
opintien kynnyksellä.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
kuule sanat suustani,  
ota virsi viereltäni.

Mieleni minun tekevi,  
aivoni ajattelevi,  
lähteäni laulamahan,  
saa’ani sanelemahan.

Sanat suustani sulavat,  
puhe’et putoelevat,  
kielelleni kerkiävät,  
hampahilleni hajoovat.

Synty syvä, synty vanha,  
tule tietä myöten tähän,  
näytä juuri, näytä alku,  
näytä oikea omasi.

Ei pahaksi, ei panoksi,  
ei kateeksi, ei kiroukseksi,  
vaan oikeaksi avuksi  
oppimisen ja ymmärryksen asiassa.

Oi Ukko, ylijumala,  
taivahallinen jumala,  
anna mielelle kirkkautta,  
anna ajatukselle selkeyttä,  
anna muistolle lujuutta,  
anna lukemiselle taitoa,  
anna kokeille onnea,  
anna opin tielle etenemistä,  
anna sana oikeahan.

Ei toisen osaa oteta,  
ei toisen onnea murreta,  
ei toisen tietä tukita,  
vaan oma mieli kirkastukoon,  
oma työ vahvistukoon,  
oma oppi kasvakoon.

Mikä on väärin lausuttu,  
se takaisin peräytyköön.  
Mikä on pahoin pantu,  
se omaan sijaansa palatkoon.  
Mikä on oikein sanottu,  
se paikalleen asettukoon.

Jos sana väärin kääntyi,  
sen nyt suustani peruutan.  
Jos voima väärään meni,  
sen nyt rauhalla palautan.  
En kiroa, en pakota,  
en syytöntä sido.

Mene väki sijallesi,  
mene voima kohdallesi,  
mene sana synnyllesi,  
mene rauha rinnalleni.

Ukko, ylijumala,  
anna anteeksi huono sana,  
anna rauha hyvään työhön,  
anna valo opin päälle.

Näin sanon, näin sidon,  
sanan suuhun, työn teloille,  
rauhan maahan, valon päälle,  
viisauden osaksi.

---

## 匈牙利 Ősmagyar Vallás

Istenem, Magyarok Istene,  
hallgasd meg e tiszta szót.

Őseim, apáim és anyáim,  
kik előttem jártatok,  
álljatok mögém tiszta emlékezettel,  
ne ártással, ne haraggal,  
hanem áldással.

Áldjon meg az Isten,  
őrizzen meg az Isten,  
fordítsa jóra a tanulás és az írás-olvasás útját.

Adjon Isten bölcsességet az elmébe,  
világosságot a gondolatba,  
jó mértéket a szóba,  
erős tartást a cselekedetbe,  
tiszta látást a döntésbe.

A Világfa rendje szerint  
gyökérből jöjjön erő,  
törzsből állhatatosság,  
ágból tágas értelem,  
levélből friss emlékezet.

A tanulás legyen szorgalmas,  
az olvasás legyen értő,  
az írás legyen rendezett,  
a vizsga útja legyen tiszta szerencsével kísért.

A zavar halkuljon,  
a félelem oldódjék,  
a szétszórt gondolat térjen vissza rendbe,  
a szív maradjon békében.

Nem kérek más kárából előmenetelt,  
nem kérek más szerencséjének elvételét,  
nem kérek rövidülést senki életére;  
csak igaz tudást, tiszta elmét,  
becsületes igyekezetet és jó eredményt kérek.

Ami ártó szó,  
ami rossz kötés,  
ami nem igaz rend szerint tapad a tanulás útjára,  
az oldódjék el,  
menjen vissza a semmibe,  
ne bántson senkit,  
ne térjen ártással.

Hálát adok az Istennek,  
hálát adok az ősök emlékezetének,  
hálát adok a kenyérért, a tűzért, a vízért,  
az otthon küszöbéért és a tiszta szóért.

Nem kérek ártást,  
nem mondok hamis esküt,  
nem gyalázom az ősöket,  
nem töröm meg a kenyeret haraggal,  
nem szennyezem a tüzet rossz szóval,  
nem veszem fel a táltos nevét igaz felhatalmazás nélkül,  
nem emelem magam más nép vagy hit fölé.

Áldás legyen a tanulás útján,  
áldás legyen az elme világosságán,  
áldás legyen azon, ami igaz és tiszta.

Úgy legyen.  
Áldás, békesség.

---

## Heathenry / Ásatrú

Friðr sé hér.  
Helga ek þenna stað til fríðar ok sannra orða.

Ek kalla á Óðin,  
Alföðr, Hroptatýr, Fimbultýr,  
rúnanna ráðanda ok leitaranda visku:  
heyr orð mín.

Heilir æsir, heilar ásynjur,  
heil sjá in fjölnýta fold!  
Mál ok manvit  
gefið okkr mærum tveim  
ok læknishendr, meðan lifum.

Ek ber fram orð, minni ok góðan hug,  
eigi til kaups, eigi til nauðungar,  
heldr til virðingar, fríðar ok rétts hugboðs.

Veit ek, at ek hekk  
vindga meiði á  
nætr allar níu,  
geiri undaðr  
ok gefinn Óðni,  
sjálfr sjálfum mér.

Ek fimbulljóð níu  
nam af inum frægja syni  
Bölþorns, Bestlu föður,  
ok ek drykk of gat  
ins dýra mjaðar,  
ausinn Óðreri.

Þá nam ek frævask  
ok fróðr vera  
ok vaxa ok vel hafask;  
orð mér af orði  
orðs leitaði,  
verk mér af verki  
verks leitaði.

Óðinn, gef mál ok manvit.  
Lát hug verða skíran, minni sterkt, orð rétt,  
lestur gagnlegan, nám vaxandi,  
ok sigr í prófraunum, ef það er rétt, heilt ok innan frithar.

Lát þann er lærir standa í frith,  
með heilum hug, heilum orðum, heilum verkum.  
Lát námsheill koma án þess at ræna öðrum heill,  
án þess at spilla hlut annarra,  
án níðs, án heiptar, án ósanns eiðs.

Ek geri eigi níð.  
Ek bind eigi vilja annars.  
Ek sver eigi ósannan eið.  
Orð mín standi innan frithar.

Óðinn, tak við þessum orðum í virðingu.  
Gef visku, skíran hug, góða námsheill ok framsókn í lærdómi,  
ef það er rétt, heilt ok innan frithar.

Svá sé.  
Friðr með oss.

---

## Maausk（爱沙尼亚）

Tere, püha hiis.  
Tere, püha maa.  
Tere, Maaema.

Mina seisan siin,  
puhta meelega  
ja rahuliku sõnaga.

Tere, esivanemad.  
Tere, isade-isade hinged.  
Tere, emade-emade hinged.  
Mäletan teid nimega ja nimeta,  
lähedalt ja kaugelt,  
oma vere, kodu ja maa kaudu.

Maaema, hoia õppijat.  
Püha hiis, hoia õppimise teed.  
Esivanemad, andke tarkust,  
andke selge meel,  
andke õiged sõnad,  
andke tugev süda.

Tulgu tarkus ja selge tee,  
kui palve on teadmise pärast:  
et õppimine kasvaks,  
raamatute sõna avaneks,  
mõte oleks klaar,  
mälu oleks kindel,  
eksamipäeval tuleks õige aeg,  
rahulik süda ja hea õnn,  
ning töö kannaks head vilja.

Ei palu ma kellegi teise õnne ära võtta,  
ei palu ma kellegi teed kitsendada,  
ei palu ma kellegi elu ega osa vähendada.  
Tulgu edu kooskõlas maa, vee, tule ja tuulega,  
ausalt, puhtalt ja õigel viisil.

Taara avita.  
Taara avita.  
Taara avita.

Katkegu segane sõna,  
vaibugu halb tahe,  
lahkugu võõras vari.  
Tulgu puhas meel,  
kindel käsi,  
õige vastus,  
rahulik tee.

Maa all rahu.  
Maa peal rahu.  
Taeva all rahu.  
Kodus rahu.  
Südames rahu.

Mis on antud, olgu puhas.  
Mis on öeldud, olgu aus.  
Mis on palutud, olgu kooskõlas  
maa, vee, tule ja tuulega.

Tänu, püha hiis.  
Tänu, Maaema.  
Tänu, esivanemad.

Kui olen eksinud sõnas või teos,  
siis peatun, puhastan oma jälje,  
võtan ära kõik sobimatu,  
ja ütlen alandliku meelega:  
andke andeks, püha paik;  
anna andeks, Maaema;  
andke andeks, esivanemad.  
Olgu see palve vaikne, aus ja puhas,  
mitte müügiks, mitte uhkuseks, mitte näitemänguks.

Taara avita.  
Nõnda olgu.

---

## 凯尔特德鲁伊（OBOD / ADF / AODA）

[净化与定界]  
Â dŵr glân, anadl dawel, a chylch o heddwch, boed y lle hwn yn bur ac yn gytûn.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[向土地与三界致敬]  
Safaf yma yn ostyngedig, heb enw personol,  
gan anrhydeddu pridd y lle hwn, dyfroedd y lle hwn, gwyntoedd y lle hwn, a thân y lle hwn.  
Anrhydedd i’r Byd Uwch, i’r Byd Canol, ac i’r Byd Is.  
Anrhydedd i ysbrydion y lle, y rhai teilwng a charedig.

[陈明目的]  
Heddiw y mae’r weddi hon dros ddoethineb wrth ddysgu, meddwl clir, cof cadarn, lwc deg mewn arholiadau, a chynnydd mewn astudiaeth.  
Na niweidied y cais hwn neb byw, na thorri rhyddid ewyllys neb, na drysu cydbwysedd tir, bodau, na chymuned.  
Ni cheisir cymryd bendith, cyfle, lwc, na ffrwyth llafur oddi wrth neb arall; ceisir goleuni cyfiawn a llwybr teg.

[分别致敬土地灵、祖灵、神明或 Awen]  
Ysbrydion y lle, derbyniwch barch pur a thawel.  
Ancestors, honoured dead, rhai a fu o’n blaenau, tystiwch y weddi hon mewn heddwch.  
Awen, ffynnon ysbrydoliaeth, llifa’n glir drwy feddwl, cof, iaith, a deall.

Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[正行：Gweddi’r Derwydd / The Druid’s Prayer]  
Dyro, Dduw, dy nawdd;  
Ac yn nawdd, nerth;  
Ac yn nerth, deall;  
Ac yn neall, gwybod;  
Ac yngwybod, gwybod y cyfiawn;  
Ac yngwybod y cyfiawn, ei garu;  
Ac o garu, caru pob hanfod;  
Ac ymhob hanfod, caru Duw;  
Duw a phob daioni.

[供献与请求]  
Boed nawdd dros y meddwl wrth agor llyfrau a dechrau gwersi.  
Boed nerth yn y corff a’r galon wrth ddyfalbarhau.  
Boed deall yn clirio dryswch, pryder, ac anghofrwydd.  
Boed gwybod yn aeddfedu’n ddoethineb, a gwybod y cyfiawn yn arwain pob ateb, dewis, ac arholiad.  
Boed Awen yn goleuo cof, rheswm, disgyblaeth, a geiriau priodol.  
Boed pob llwyddiant yn deg, yn onest, ac yn llesol.

Rhoddir dŵr glân, neu ronyn o fara neu had, i’r ddaear mewn diolchgarwch.  
Nid fel cyfnewid na gorfodaeth y rhoddir, ond fel parch i’r tir a’r rhai caredig sy’n tystio.

[静默承接]  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[感谢诸灵]  
Diolch i’r ddaear dan draed.  
Diolch i ysbrydion y lle.  
Diolch i’r hynafiaid anrhydeddus.  
Diolch i Awen, ffynnon y goleuni mewn dysg a deall.  
Bydded i bob un ddychwelyd i’w le mewn heddwch ac urddas.

[关闭与回归]  
Y weddi a lefarwyd; boed iddi agor yn unig mewn ffyrdd cyfiawn, caredig, a chytûn.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

---

## Kemetism

ỉw=ỉ r ḏd mdw m mꜣꜥt.  
ỉb=ỉ wꜥb, r=ỉ mꜣꜥ, ḏrt=ỉ wꜥbt.  
n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḥḏ ḥtpw nṯrw.  
n ỉnk šd mꜣꜥt.

dwꜣ Ḏḥwty.  
dwꜣ Ḏḥwty, sš n nṯrw, nb mdw-nṯr.  
ỉꜣw n=k, Ḏḥwty, nb sš, nb sjꜣ, nb mḏꜣt.  
di=k mꜣꜥt r st=s, di=k ḥtp r ỉb.

ḥtp dỉ nsw Ḏḥwty nb Ḫmnw.  
dỉ=f prt-ḫrw:  
t ḥnqt, kꜣw ꜣpdw, šs mnḫt,  
snṯr mrḥt, ḫt nb(t) nfr(t) wꜥb(t),  
n kꜣ n sḫr m mꜣꜥt.

ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
ỉb=ỉ n ḫprw=ỉ,  
m ḏd r=ỉ m mꜣꜥty,  
m ỉr ḫft r=ỉ m-bꜣḥ nṯr ꜥꜣ.  
ỉb=ỉ n mwt=ỉ,  
m ḫsf r=ỉ m ḏꜣḏꜣt.

n ỉnk ỉr ỉsft.  
n ỉnk ḏd grg.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n nṯr.  
n ỉnk ỉṯỉ ḫt n ꜣḫ.  
n ỉnk ḥtm rn.  
n ỉnk sḫm r ḏrt ḫft mꜣꜥt.
